## people magazine collage cover

![people magazine collage cover](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/829.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@qisi_ai](https://x.com/qisi_ai/status/1999057085624164607)
- **Tags:** nature, portrait, typography

**Prompt:**

```
1. Overall goal
1 Function description: Based on the character reference picture uploaded by the user, extract the character's temperament, makeup style, light and color characteristics to create a unique fashion portrait collage.
2 Difference requirements: retain the facial structure and overall temperament of the reference character, do not directly copy the original picture, and make creative changes in makeup and composition within the same style system.

2. Enter the reference drawing requirements
1 Reference content: A clear front-face or two-thirds profile photo of a person, where the facial features, skin texture, and general lighting atmosphere can be seen clearly.
2 Extract key points: Read the skin color, makeup shade, main color, light direction, character temperament and clothing color matching from the reference picture.

3. Screen composition and output form
1 Main picture: Generate a super close-up or close-up view of the character's face. The head and shoulders occupy most of the space in the picture. The line of sight can refer to the temperament design of the original picture.
2 Collage structure: Add multiple small picture collages on the right side or one corner, which can include close-ups of side faces, hands, partial makeup, etc., to create a magazine layout feel.
3. Background method: Keep the background simple and clean, using solid colors or slight transitions of brightness to highlight the characters and makeup.

4. Text and graphic design
1 Title text: Place a large magazine title at the top of the screen. The font should be simple and powerful. Keep it centered or aligned at the top.
2 Subtitles and small fonts: Add a few lines of small fonts on the side or bottom of the screen. The content can be subject words, character names, dates, arranged neatly, and the font size is uniform.
3 Geometric shapes: Add thin lines, narrow rectangular color blocks or translucent color blocks around the characters, and use them in conjunction with text to increase the sense of plane composition.

5. Style inheritance rules
1 Color inheritance: The overall tone, light and dark contrast, and warm and cold temperament should fit the style of the reference picture as much as possible. The main color comes from the most conspicuous makeup or clothing color in the reference picture.
2 Light inheritance: Refer to the light direction and softness of the original image. If the original image is soft light, maintain the soft light texture. If the original image has strong contrast, retain a certain toughness.
3 Makeup inheritance: Keep the same style level according to the makeup characteristics of the reference picture (clear, intense, experimental, natural, etc.), and then make detailed changes in eye makeup, blush, and lip makeup.
4. Atmosphere inheritance: Continuing the emotional atmosphere of the reference picture, such as coldness, sweetness, rebellion, mystery, etc., echoing it in expressions and postures.

6. Creative change rules
1. Makeup changes: Add local exaggeration based on the reference style, such as expanding the blush range, strengthening lip blending, adding freckles or highlights.
2. Composition changes: You can adjust the face angle, cropping range and small picture collage position, so that each generation has a different composition.
3. Changes in accessories: Add simple and stylish accessories to the neck, ears or hands, echoing the main color but not completely replicating the reference picture.
4 Detailed gestures: Add hand movements such as touching lips, cheeks, and eyes to make the picture more story-telling and engaging.

7. Overall texture and later style
1. Clarity: Keep skin pores and details visible, avoid excessive dermabrasion, but soften out-of-focus areas appropriately.
2. Color tone processing: The overall color tone is unified, the cluttered colors are moderately reduced, and only the main color and a few embellishment colors are strengthened.
3. Emotional expression: According to the temperament of the reference picture, control the intensity of expressions and eyes, so that the picture retains the original style and has an independent personality.

Refer to the photos of people uploaded by users, automatically read the image style and create according to the above rules.
```

## Dongshan Xiaohong

![Dongshan Xiaohong](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/835.jpeg)

- **Source:** [@qisi_ai](https://x.com/qisi_ai/status/1999109193652113499)
- **Tags:** animal, architecture, fashion, landscape, nature, portrait, vehicle

**Prompt:**

```
1. Overall atmosphere
1 Scene setting: daily outdoor life, residential road, white fence, green plant background, sunny daylight
2. Picture temperament: fresh, quiet, slightly cute, Japanese youthful, slightly two-dimensional.
3 Color tone: main color of black and white, white skin color, bright red accessories, overall soft contrast of warm and cold

2. Character image
1 Age image: Delicate and cute face, large eyes, a small mole under the right eye, light pink lips, clean Japanese and Korean makeup, girlish look, slender figure, childish face, delicate skin
2 Hairstyle, expression and posture: Dongshan Xiaohong from the cosplayer Chainsaw Man, standing frontally with both hands raised to make scissor hands

3. Clothing style
1 Top: black loose jacket, plush lapels, front zipper design, slightly puffy hem and cuffs
2 Pattern elements: There are graffiti patterns such as fish bones, crosses, and simple animal drawings on the jacket, giving it a sense of dark childishness.
3 Inner wear: Light-colored round-neck top, revealing a small amount of neckline to create a contrast between light and dark.
4 accessories: red choker, metal buckle, long cross earrings, red hairpins worn in groups
5 style tags: street cute style, soft and slightly rebellious mix, subculture girl outfits

4. Composition and camera position
1. Composition method: the character is in the center, half-body framing, upper body and gestures are the visual focus.
2 Camera viewing angle: slightly overhead, close to human eye height, moderate distance
3 Spatial relationship: There is a certain distance between the character and the background fence, and the background is slightly blurred to highlight the subject.

5. Light, shadow and texture
1 Light source: natural sunlight, illumination from the front and side, even light on the face
2. The relationship between light and dark: the character is overall bright, the background is slightly dark and there are shaded areas, forming a soft contrast.
3 Texture performance: The plush collar has a clear texture, the jacket has a soft suede surface, and the metal jewelry has small highlights.

6. Environmental elements
1 Background buildings: metal gates, distant residential walls, local vehicles and stone pillars
2 Surrounding details: white wooden fence, stone road, slight water stains and fallen leaves on the ground
3 Atmosphere keywords: quiet residential area, relaxing walking scene, slightly winter or early spring atmosphere
```

## Ancient style wide-sleeved robe garden night scene photo

![Ancient style wide-sleeved robe garden night scene photo](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/841.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@qisi_ai](https://x.com/qisi_ai/status/1999333876033049003)
- **Tags:** landscape, nature, portrait

**Prompt:**

```
1. Screen composition and camera position
1 Screen ratio: Vertical composition, characters occupy about four-fifths of the height of the screen
2 Lens distance: medium and close shot, completely in the frame from the knees to the top of the head
3. Camera height: slightly lower than the person’s line of sight.
4. Character position: The center of the screen is slightly upward, and the body is slightly tilted to the right.
5. White space in the picture: a small amount of white space at the top and bottom, and the left and right sides are surrounded by dark night scenes and wooden railings.
6 Supplementary image quality: For example, in a low-quality iPhone photo taken with flash under dim light, the background is almost completely black and nothing can be seen clearly.

2. Scene and environment
1 Scene type: Ancient garden night scene

3. Character setting and posture
1 Character setting: delicate face, large eyes, a small mole under the right eye, slender nose, light pink lips, clean makeup, Japanese and Korean style.
2 Postures and movements: Sitting on a wooden bench with arms placed naturally
3. Shoulder and neck lines: Expose shoulders and collarbones in large areas, and the neck is slender.
4. Facial angle: facing the camera, head slightly tilted forward, expression calm and relaxed

4. Clothing styling
1 Clothing style: Ancient style wide-sleeved robe with light-colored laces and dark patterns. The neckline is slanted and the large neckline naturally slides down to expose the collarbone, shoulder and neck lines.
5. Shawl structure
1 Shawl structure: Soft and fluffy white plush shawl, slides down and wraps around the forearms and knees, forming a full circle of plush enveloping feeling, with soft and fluffy edges and small plush details.

6. Hair style
1. Hair style: tall ancient-style updo, high bun, fluffy and bulging top, round and full bun, hair at the back is gathered and coiled, hair on both sides is combed back and fixed, the overall outline is long and oval, the hairline is clean and tidy, long sideburns are left on both sides of the cheeks, falling straight to the waist, close to the face and modifying the face shape.

7. Accessories
1 Accessories: Pairs of ancient-style walking hair accessories, worn symmetrically on both sides of the bun. Metallic hair forks are inserted into the top of the bun, connecting multiple layers of tassels and pendants. Thin chains hang down in layers, with small beads and small flower-shaped metal pieces. There are drop-shaped pendants in some parts. As the head moves slightly, the metal and pearls have obvious highlights in the night. The overall look is gorgeous but not overly exaggerated.

8. Hair texture and direction
1 Hair texture and direction: Natural black straight hair, the hair is fine and smooth, with a slight soft shine. The temple hair close to the face hangs down tightly, with straight and clean lines. The part of the hair is rolled up to closely fit the head shape. There are a few strands of fine hair on the edges that spread out softly. The overall hair volume is large, the outline is clear, and there are real hair texture and slight frizzy details.

9. Expression of emotions and atmosphere
1. Emotional tone: quiet, gentle, slightly distant but also close.
2 Atmosphere setting: Late at night in the garden, the surroundings are quiet, the air is cold, and the characters give people a soft and safe feeling.
3 Eye interaction: look directly at the camera, no exaggerated smile, subtle eyes, convey gentle and calm emotions
```

## 9-square grid nude 3D collage poster

![9-square grid nude 3D collage poster](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/848.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@langzihan](https://x.com/langzihan/status/2000416971662479749)
- **Tags:** 3d, character, fashion, futuristic, logo, minimalist, neon, photography, portrait, poster, typography

**Prompt:**

```
# Role: Fashion Art Director & Prompt Engineer

## 1. Mission objectives
Your current task is to design a set of advanced AI drawing prompts (Prompts) for generating "multi-cover fashion magazine collage posters" based on the [target object/person] provided by the user. You need to replicate a specific visual structure: the background is composed of multiple magazine cover-style grids, and there is a central character in the foreground that breaks the borders to create an "out of the box" three-dimensional visual effect.

## 2. Image structure framework (Structure & Layout Analysis)
Please strictly implement the following visual framework in the generated prompt:
* **Composition mode**: Magazine Grid Collage (magazine collage grid) / Bento Box Style (lunch box layout).
* **Background layer**: Divide the screen into 7-9 rectangular areas. Each area mimics the cover of a top fashion magazine (Vogue, Bazaar, Elle, i-D, Dazed, GQ, Marie Claire, etc.).
* **Foreground layer (emphasis)**: Generate a Full Body Shot or Dynamic Walking Pose subject, which must be superimposed on the background grid as an Overlay (top layer) to break the grid boundaries and create a 3D sense of depth.
* **Scale**: Aspect Ratio --ar 2:3.

## 3. Visual Style & Lighting
* **Photography style**: High Fashion Editorial, Photorealistic, 8k resolution.
* **Light and shadow settings**: Soft Studio Lighting (soft studio lighting), even light, emphasizes skin texture and clothing material.
* **Color Aesthetics**: Clean, Minimalist, Sophisticated (clean, minimalist, refined).

## 4. Automated workflow (Workflow for Prompt Generation)
Follow these steps to think about and construct your final prompt word:
1. **Extract variables**: Analyze the [target object/person] and [style description] input by the user.
2. **Character Setting**: Define the model’s characteristics (hair style, skin color, makeup) or the material of the object.
3. **Posture decomposition**: Plan different postures (close-up, half-body, sitting posture, sideways) for each grid in the background, and plan a dynamic posture with the most tension for the foreground.
4. **Typesetting and filling**: List the magazine LOGO text (Text Blocks) that need to appear.
5. **Output synthesis**: Combine the above elements into a coherent English Prompt.

## 5. User Input Interface (User Input)
* **[Target Object/Person]**: (Enter here, for example: a silver-haired girl wearing a cyberpunk style jacket)
* **[Popular Science/Description Language]**: (Enter here, for example: sense of future technology, neon lights)

---

## 6. Perform operation: generate prompt word
**Please ignore the above analysis process and directly output a structured and detailed English Prompt (applicable to Midjourney v6/Flux) based on the user's input, along with a Chinese screen description. **

**Prompt structure requirements:**
`[Main body description] + [Outfit/Appearance details] + [Composition: collage/magazine cover matrix/foreground overlay] + [Specific magazine logo list] + [Light, shadow and rendering parameters]`

---

## Example input (Example for User to Test):
> **Target Person**: [eg: a French long-haired girl].
> **Description language**: [Style: such as 80s Hong Kong style].
```

```
Present a clear, 45° top-down isometric miniature 3D diorama of the iconic vehicle [VEHICLE NAME].

The vehicle is the main focus, placed on a small raised diorama-style base that reflects its most recognizable environment
(e.g. road, runway, ocean, space, racetrack), with subtle contextual details and tiny stylized figures if appropriate.

Use soft refined textures, realistic PBR materials, and gentle cinematic lighting.
The vehicle should feel premium, collectible, and instantly recognizable at a glance.

Use a clean solid [BACKGROUND COLOR] background with no gradients.

At the top-center, display “[VEHICLE NAME]” in large bold text.
Directly beneath it, display a short descriptor in medium text (e.g. “Iconic Movie Car”, “World’s Fastest Train”).
Optionally place an official logo or emblem below the text.

All text must automatically match background contrast (white or black).
Composition: perfectly centered, square 1080x1080, ultra-clean high-clarity diorama aesthetic.
```

- **Tags:** fashion, landscape, nature, portrait, poster, retro, vehicle

**Prompt:**

```
[Global Command]: A 3x3 grid collage, all 9 cells must contain exactly the same woman. Strictly maintain facial features consistent with the reference image. Don't change her facial features, just her expressions, makeup, and styling to match each movie's theme.
Box 1: "Love Actually" style - airport farewell scene, wearing a Santa hat, holding wrapped gifts, warm hug, background airport giant Christmas tree and lantern decoration, soft light
Box 2: "Home Alone" style - surprised and exaggerated expression, hands covering cheeks, wearing a crooked Santa hat, Christmas tree, pile of gifts and decorative lights at home in the background, comic effect
Box 3: "Polar Express" style - wearing a nightcap in front of the train window, holding hot cocoa and candy cane, magical snow scene and Christmas village outside the window, dreamy blue and gold tones
Box 4: "How the Grinch Stole Christmas" style - real characters in green costumes and red Christmas hats, funny expressions, holding stolen Christmas decorations, Christmas village lights and gifts in the background, creative styling
Box 5: Miracle on 34th Street style - retro department store scene wearing classic red Christmas dress, holding Christmas shopping bags, giant Christmas tree and retro decorations in the background, classic Hollywood lighting (center)
Box 6: "Christmas Elf" style - complete elf costume (green top, red striped socks, pointed hat with bells), jumping happily, holding a candy cane, candy-colored Christmas workshop in the background
Box 7: "Frozen" style - ice blue princess dress with snowflake crown, holding magic ice crystals, snowflakes flying, ice crystal castle and big Christmas tree in the background, special festive candies, Disney magic feeling
Box 8: "True Lies" style - black dress with red Christmas ornaments, holding champagne, Christmas party scene lights and decorative balls in the background, elegant and mysterious
Grid 9: "Last Christmas" style - a fashionable woman wearing a red retro coat with a green scarf and gold earrings, holding a Christmas gift box, standing under the lights of the London Christmas market, with the giant Christmas tree and holiday windows of Covent Garden in the background, warm night lights, hopeful expressions, modern romantic movie aesthetics
Each frame imitates the tone, light and atmosphere of the corresponding movie, with extremely obvious Christmas decoration elements, movie poster composition, adding movie-like title text effects, professional movie stills texture, 4K high definition
```

## Photos of Victorian Gothic Royal Family

![Photos of Victorian Gothic Royal Family](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/904.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@songguoxiansen](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2001828831615946768)
- **Tags:** architecture, fashion, landscape, nature, paper-craft, photography, portrait, typography, ui

**Prompt:**

```
Generate a 9:16 vertical version of the realistic photo of "Victorian Gothic Royal Family": use the FACE_REF I uploaded as a reference for the character's identity, 100% restoration of facial features and bones; the character is wearing a heavy-duty dress (corset, large bustle, lace/velvet, royal jewelry) in the "Victorian Era (19th century) court dress direction", and was photographed next to Tower Bridge in London or the Palace of Westminster (Big Ben). The picture has the photography, styling and cover design of "Harper’s Bazaar", maintaining the magazine’s consistent design style (Chinese and English design).

【INPUTS | input】
FACE_REF: The facial features reference picture I uploaded (identity locked)

[ABSOLUTE PRIORITY | Identity lock (highest priority)]
100% restoration of FACE_REF's facial features and bone structure: the distance between the eyes, the bridge of the nose, the lip shape, the mandible line, and the cheekbone structure are completely consistent and must not drift.
Real skin texture: Visible fine texture and pores, don’t over-skin the skin and become internet celebrity.
The image of an adult female.

[SHOT TYPE | Choose one of two scenes (one is randomly selected by the model, and must be real and unified)]
A) Half-body cover: from chest to waist, jewelry, lace neckline and eyes are the clearest (main recommendation)
B) Full-body cover: From head to toe, the huge skirt silhouette is completely displayed, combining it with London landmarks, with a strong sense of perspective (optional)
(Regardless of A/B: the "cover composition" must be maintained, with blank space for typesetting, but no torn paper/hand-painted effect.)

【LOCATION | Scene (London, UK)】
London landmarks: the banks of the River Thames, with the magnificent Gothic Palace of Westminster (Big Ben) or the towers of Tower Bridge in the background.
Choose one of two weather conditions (randomly): 1) London fog (classic foggy texture, soft and mysterious light) 2) Overcast and rainy (the ground is wet and reflective, the sky is leaden gray)
The background is clean: no tourists, no modern logos, no mobile status bar UI, no watermarked subtitles.

【LIGHTING & CAMERA | Photographic quality (magazine level)】
Lens feel: 85mm portrait texture (half body) or 50mm/70mm (full body), shallow depth of field, the clearest eyes.
Light: cloudy diffused light + dramatic fill light (emphasis on facial structure); diamonds/gems have real fire; velvet texture is deep.
Color: High-end cinematic feel. The low-saturation blue-gray environment color and the dark tones of the clothing (red/blue/black) form a Gothic aesthetic; the whole is clean, transparent and noble.

[WARDROBE | Victoria court dress (heavy work, shaping, complicated details)]
Target aesthetic: "wasp waist, big skirt, layered lace, heavy velvet, crown, queenly aura".

Silhouette and layering (X-shaped tailoring)
Upper body: Corset with strong structure, square collar or high collar, puff sleeves or leg-of-mutton sleeves
Lower body: Huge bustle (Crinoline or Bustle), obvious stacking design at the back waist, floor-length skirt
Decoration: Lots of ruffles, bows, draped tassels
Fabrics and craftsmanship (valuing craftsmanship must be “visible”)
Main fabric: heavy velvet, taffeta, Chantilly Lace
Main crafts: bead embroidery, gold thread embroidery, ribbon weaving
Pattern themes: Damask, rose, thistle (Scottish symbol), paisley
Details: Lace gloves, choker, medal/brooch
Head and face (royal jewelry and headwear)
Core structure: Victorian small crown (Tiara) or feather headdress
Decoration: diamonds, sapphires, pearls
Earrings/Neck Jewelry: Extremely exaggerated diamond necklaces and earrings

[COLOR MATRIX | Color matrix matching (must be executed, and must be "royal dark")]
(Late Victorian deep luxury)
Randomly select 1 set from the following three sets of "main color schemes" as the [base color/large-area main fabric color].

Scheme G (royal blue background):
Base color: deep sapphire blue/midnight blue (velvet texture)
Embroidery/embroidery: silver lace, diamonds, sapphires
Scheme A (Victoria red bottom):
Base color: burgundy/burgundy (deep and passionate)
Embroidery/Embroidery: Black lace, gold embroidery, rubies
Scheme R (mourning black bottom):
Base color: Black Jet (extreme goth)
Embroidery/Decoration: Black beading, black lace, a small amount of gold or silver highlights

[Color execution rules]
The color should be deep and rich, reflecting the majesty of "the sun never sets" and the mystery of Gothic.

[POSE | Cover posture (majestic, stiff, queenly)]
Half body: chin slightly raised, eyes cold, one hand caressing the necklace
Whole body: Standing tall and straight (like a portrait), hands folded on the bustle, overwhelming aura
Expression: Serious, arrogant, arrogant; never smile (Victorian style).

[OUTPUT | Output]
1 9:16 vertical realistic magazine cover photo
Random: half body or whole body (choose one from A/B)
Random: fog or rain (choose one of the two weather conditions)
Randomly: sapphire blue / burgundy / jet black (choose one from three color matrix)
Look: Victorian Court Dress Directions + Tiara/Choker + Busty Bust + Velvet Lace
```

## Take selfies with characters from movies and TV shows

```
Create a realistic first-person POV selfie as if the camera is my own eyes using a phone’s front-facing camera. The phone, my hands, and my arms must NOT be visible in the frame. Use the uploaded image as my identity reference and keep my face recognizable through perspective consistency. I am not part of the cast I’m a guest on set wearing modern, casual real-world clothing that does not match the actors’ wardrobe. The actors are aware of the selfie, standing very close to me, leaning in naturally, and looking directly into the camera as if pausing for a quick friendly shot between takes. 

The framing should feel intimate and face-level, with actors filling the foreground. The background must clearly show a believable behind-the-scenes film set with cameras, crew, lighting rigs, monitors, and equipment. The image should feel candid, unpolished, and spontaneous.
```

## A duo of specimen boxes and realistic outfit aesthetics

![A duo of specimen boxes and realistic outfit aesthetics](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/908.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@LufzzLiz](https://x.com/LufzzLiz/status/2001831802269499412)
- **Tags:** cartoon, fashion, paper-craft, photography, portrait, product, retro, vehicle

**Prompt:**

```
A vertical split-screen creative product photography composition on a clean white wall background. High-resolution, photorealistic, commercial advertisement quality.

Top Section: The Specimen Box
The upper half features an exquisite light oak wooden shadow box frame mounted on the wall. Inside, a specific outfit is displayed as an artistic flat-lay museum specimen: [Insert Clothing Details Here, e.g., a sleek black satin slip dress with delicate lace trim and thin spaghetti straps]. Elegant calligraphy on the matte paper backdrop reads: [Insert Text, e.g., "Midnight Elegance" or "Silk & Secrets"]. Soft studio lighting accentuates the rich texture and drape of the fabric.

Bottom Section: Naked-Eye 3D Reality
The lower half creates a hyperrealistic "naked-eye 3D" illusion. A rectangular picture-frame border sits directly beneath the top box. A stunningly realistic young woman [Insert Model Description, e.g., a poised East Asian model with long wavy black hair, subtle smoky eyes, and a confident gaze] wears the exact same outfit as shown above.

She lounges casually on the bottom edge of the frame—one leg bent with foot resting inside the frame, the other leg elegantly dangling out into the viewer’s space. Her torso leans back slightly, elbow resting on her raised knee, fingers lightly grazing the fabric near her collarbone. Her body forms a soft, sensual S-curve that highlights the garment’s silhouette without overt exposure. She looks directly at the camera with a calm, knowing smile—inviting yet enigmatic. This dynamic, lifelike pose contrasts powerfully with the static, archival display above, creating visual tension between reality and presentation.

Technical Specs:
Soft natural shadows, ambient occlusion, bright and airy yet cinematic lighting, 8K resolution, Octane Render, vivid but refined color palette, ultra-detailed fabric textures (satin sheen, lace transparency, stitching), shallow depth of field, Vogue editorial style, filmic grain, professional fashion photography.

Negative Prompt (recommended):
blurry, low-res, distorted anatomy, extra limbs, deformed hands, cartoon, anime, doll-like, plastic skin, overexposed, cluttered background, text errors, mismatched clothing, floating objects, unrealistic proportions.
Reference character, I want to see the teacher’s uniform
```

```
The couple appears natural, affectionate, and playful, captured in multiple candid moments as if taken inside a photo booth. The woman and the man maintain their original facial features, skin tones, and expressions.
Woman: elegant, feminine, glowing skin, natural makeup, soft blush, glossy lips, long dark hair styled loosely with gentle volume. Wearing a minimal strapless cream or light beige dress.
Man: clean and handsome appearance, short dark hair, light stubble or clean-shaven, wearing a black leather jacket over a white shirt
Scenes & poses included in the collage:
The woman smiling brightly while the man stands behind her playfully covering her eyes.
The couple standing close, facing each other lovingly, her hand resting on his chest.
A close face-to-face moment with soft smiles and eye contact.
The woman standing behind the man, making a peace sign while smiling at the camera.
A playful dancing pose where the man lifts one of the woman’s hands as if spinning her.
A relaxed, candid moment where both laugh naturally at the camera.
Environment: neutral photo booth backdrop with soft vertical curtains, warm indoor lighting, subtle shadows, cozy and intimate atmosphere.
Photography style: vintage Polaroid / analog photo booth aesthetic, slightly soft focus, gentle grain, mild blur, natural imperfections, warm tones, realistic skin texture.
Lighting: soft frontal flash combined with ambient light, creating a casual, real-life snapshot feeling.
Mood & vibe: romantic, playful, spontaneous, intimate, youthful, nostalgic.
Composition: multi-frame vertical collage, evenly spaced images, authentic photo booth layout.
Quality: high realism, not AI-looking, natural proportions, no distortion.
```

## Turn your favorite characters into collectibles

![Turn your favorite characters into collectibles](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/945.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@Gdgtify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2002116477307044203)
- **Tags:** character, landscape, logo, minimalist, nature, portrait, poster, product, toy

**Prompt:**

```
do this for Messi: <instruction>
Relic-Loadout Kit
Input A is a fictional or real character (image/name) OR story IP (poster/name).
Analyze and infer: character archetype, iconic scene, signature items, and moral arc.
Goal: Premium collector kit box with compartments (no logos; minimal text).
Rules:
Center compartment: mini figurine.
Surround 10–16 relic props that teach the character arc (before/after item, symbol of sacrifice, tool of choice).
Add a tiny “arc timeline” strip with 5 beats (icons + 1–2 words max each).
Output: one image, 4:5 product hero shot.
</instruction>
```

---

## Christmas special - characters frozen in fantasy giant glass snow globes

![Christmas special - characters frozen in fantasy giant glass snow globes](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/947.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@songguoxiansen](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2002370189384691980)
- **Tags:** character, fantasy, interior, landscape, nature, photography, portrait

**Prompt:**

```
(Surrealism, fantasy art, macro photography style). A magical composition where the specific character is captured inside a giant, life-sized glass snow globe. [CRITICAL: Keep the face identical to the source image, maintain consistent facial features within the glass distortion].

Inside the Globe: The character is wearing a white faux fur winter coat and a red Santa hat, catching falling snowflakes with her hands. The environment inside includes miniature snow-covered pine trees decorated with colorful Christmas lights twinkling in red, green, blue, and gold. A tiny wooden cabin sits among the trees. Swirling magical glitter and snow dust fill the air inside the sphere.

Outside the Globe: The background is a blurry, cozy living room with a fireplace, emphasizing that the character is inside the ornament.

Lighting: The snow globe is glowing from within, illuminated by the warm colorful glow of the Christmas tree lights mixing with cool magical blue and white light on the falling snow. The character's face is beautifully lit by this magical mixed lighting. External warm light reflects off the curved glass surface, creating rainbow prismatic effects.

Technical: Ray tracing reflections on the glass, refraction effects, crystal clear focus on the character, magical atmosphere, ethereal and dreamy aesthetic, 8k resolution, intricate details of the snowflakes and Christmas lights bokeh.
```

## Christmas Special - Christmas Fashion with Red Rhyme

![Christmas Special - Christmas Fashion with Red Rhyme](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/949.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@songguoxiansen](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2002735852284457029)
- **Tags:** character, fashion, minimalist, nature, paper-craft, portrait, vehicle

**Prompt:**

```
(Magazine cover layout, minimalist composition, negative space). A full-body studio shot of the specific character sitting on a tall stool. [CRITICAL: Ensure the face is exactly the same as the reference].

Styling: Minimalist chic outfit (black turtleneck, jeans). A long red scarf flowing down. Wearing subtle reindeer antlers. Props: A single red Christmas bauble hanging from a string right above her hand. Snowflake light patterns projected on the background wall. Background: Solid light grey or white seamless paper. Lighting: Soft, directional light creating a clean look with defined shadows. Style: Vogue or Elle magazine style, high fashion, clean lines, modern and sophisticated.
```

## Christmas Special - My Christmas is in tune with myself

![Christmas Special - My Christmas is in tune with myself](https://opennana.com/awesome-prompt-gallery/images/950.jpeg)

- **Model:** Nano banana pro
- **Source:** [@songguoxiansen](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2002382591823896676)
- **Tags:** character, photography, portrait

**Prompt:**

```
(2-panel vertical split, twin concept, studio photography). Two panels side-by-side showing the specific character interacting with the frame edge (as if looking at herself). [CRITICAL: Keep the face identical to the source image in both panels].

Left Panel: Wearing a green sweater and Santa hat, holding a Christmas cracker ready to pull, leaning right.
Right Panel: Wearing a red sweater, holding the other end of the Christmas cracker, leaning left. Surrounded by Christmas lights.
Props: Wrapped gifts and a snowman doll at their feet.
Background: Yellow or teal bright studio background.
Lighting: Flat, bright, shadowless lighting.
Style: Fun, creative, "cloning" effect, playful narrative.
aspect_ratio: 16:9
```
